	declare last_rand_value : int := 0
	declare read randNoteValues[128] : int[]
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(randNoteValues) - 1)) 
		non_rpt_random(randNoteValues[i], last_rand_value, 0, 1000)
		randNoteValues[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(randNoteValues[i]) - 0) * (500 - - 500)) / (1000 - 0)) + - 500)
		inc(i)
	end while

	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_vibIntensity), CONTROL_PAR_PARENT_PANEL, get_ui_id(UI_vibrato))
	declare const tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS : int := real_to_int(int_to_real(257) / 2.056)
	declare tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : real[]
	declare tbl_rate.expCurve[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_rate.logCurve[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_rate.linCurve[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_rate.decayCurve[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_rate.releaseCurve[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_rate.attack : real
	declare tbl_rate.attack_idx : int
	declare tbl_rate.hold : int
	declare tbl_rate.decay : real
	declare tbl_rate.sustain : int
	declare tbl_rate.release : real
	declare tbl_rate.curve : int
	declare tbl_rate.release_idx : int
	declare tbl_rate.attack_point : real
	declare ui_table tbl_rate1[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[] (2, 2, 1000)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(tbl_rate1), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate1), CONTROL_PAR_BAR_COLOR, 16711679)

	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate1), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envRateCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - 40)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate1), CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 257)

	declare ui_table tbl_rate2[tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[] (2, 2, 1000)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_BAR_COLOR, 16711679)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_ZERO_LINE_COLOR, 16711679)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_VALUE)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_Z_LAYER, - 1)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envRateCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 12) + 1)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envRateCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - 40)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 257)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, 40)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate1), CONTROL_PAR_PARENT_PANEL, get_ui_id(UI_vibrato))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_rate2), CONTROL_PAR_PARENT_PANEL, get_ui_id(UI_vibrato))
	declare const tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS : int := real_to_int(int_to_real(257) / 2.056)
	declare tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : real[]
	declare tbl_int.expCurve[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_int.logCurve[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_int.linCurve[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_int.decayCurve[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_int.releaseCurve[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[]
	declare tbl_int.attack : real
	declare tbl_int.attack_idx : int
	declare tbl_int.hold : int
	declare tbl_int.decay : real
	declare tbl_int.sustain : int
	declare tbl_int.release : real
	declare tbl_int.curve : int
	declare tbl_int.release_idx : int
	declare tbl_int.attack_point : real
	declare ui_table tbl_int1[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[] (2, 2, 1000)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_BAR_COLOR, 16711679)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_ZERO_LINE_COLOR, 16711679)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_VALUE)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_Z_LAYER, - 1)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envIntCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 12)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envIntCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - 40)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 257)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, 40)
	declare ui_table tbl_int2[tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS] : int[] (2, 2, 1000)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_BAR_COLOR, 16711679)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_ZERO_LINE_COLOR, 16711679)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_VALUE)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_Z_LAYER, - 1)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envIntCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 12) + 1)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_envIntCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) - 40)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, 257)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, 40)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int1), CONTROL_PAR_PARENT_PANEL, get_ui_id(UI_vibrato))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(tbl_int2), CONTROL_PAR_PARENT_PANEL, get_ui_id(UI_vibrato))
	tbl_rate.curve := sli_envRateCurve
	tbl_rate.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_rate.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_rate.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold := (((sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain := (((sli_envRateSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.decay) - ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_rate.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_rate.sustain
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.release) - ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.attack_idx := search(tbl_rate.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_rate.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[(((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_rate.curve < 500000)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i - (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_rate.release_idx)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i - tbl_rate.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_rate1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_rate2[i] := tbl_rate1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.curve := sli_envIntCurve
	tbl_int.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_int.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_int.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_int.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_int.hold := (((sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_int.sustain := (((sli_envIntSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_int.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.decay) - ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_int.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_int.sustain
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.release) - ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.attack_idx := search(tbl_int.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_int.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[(((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold))
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.decayCurve[i - (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_int.release_idx)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i - tbl_int.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_int1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_int2[i] := tbl_int1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while

	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_lock), CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, 20)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_lock), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31)) - 1, 31))])
	set_key_pressed_support(0)
	update.keycolor()
	if(not (- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1))
		all_windows.show(FALSE)
		btn_home := TRUE
		home.show(btn_home)
	end if
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_home), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31)])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_legatoSettings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31)])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_vibratoSettings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31)])
end on

on persistence_changed
	if(pgs_init = 0)
		pgs_init := 1
		load.arrays()
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_loadedData), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legato_prefixes[prefix_idx])
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(txt_loadedData), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legato_prefixes[prefix_idx])
		if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
			all_windows.show(FALSE)
			btn_legatoSettings := TRUE
			legatoSettings.show(btn_legatoSettings)
		end if
		call update.cc_dynamics()
		call update.cc_expression()
		call update.cc_vibrato()
		if(not in_range(trans_idx, 0, search(trans_zone_ids, - 1)))
			play_event := range[0]
			play_velo := 1
		else
			if(1 = TRUE)
				play_event := lsb(trans_zone_ids[element.idx])
				play_velo := msb(trans_zone_ids[element.idx])
			else
				play_event := get_zone_par(trans_zone_ids[element.idx], ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
				play_velo := get_zone_par(trans_zone_ids[element.idx], ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
			end if
		end if
		event_note := play_event
		if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
			call update.waveform()
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_noInput), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			call update.legatoArrays()
			update.legatoList()
		end if
	end if
end on

on listener
	if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
		if((NI_SIGNAL_TYPE = NI_SIGNAL_TIMER_MS) and (pgs_init = 1))
			if(event_status(transition_id) # EVENT_STATUS_INACTIVE)
				set_ui_wf_property(get_ui_id(wf_transition), UI_WF_PROP_PLAY_CURSOR, 0, get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS))
			else
				if(event_status(play_id) # EVENT_STATUS_INACTIVE)
					btn_play := TRUE
					set_ui_wf_property(get_ui_id(wf_transition), UI_WF_PROP_PLAY_CURSOR, 0, get_event_par(play_id, EVENT_PAR_PLAY_POS))
				end if
			end if
			if((btn_play = TRUE) and (event_status(play_id) = EVENT_STATUS_INACTIVE))
				btn_play := FALSE
				set_ui_wf_property(get_ui_id(wf_transition), UI_WF_PROP_PLAY_CURSOR, 0, HIDE_PART_CURSOR)
			end if
		end if
	end if
end on

on controller
	if(CC_NUM = num_dynamic_cc)
		sli_dynamics := real_to_int((((int_to_real(CC[num_dynamic_cc]) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (127 - 0)) + 0)
		call update.cc_dynamics()
	end if
	if(CC_NUM = 111)
		sli_expression := real_to_int((((int_to_real(CC[111]) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (127 - 0)) + 0)
		call update.cc_expression()
	end if
	if(CC_NUM = 101)
		sli_vibrato := real_to_int((((int_to_real(CC[101]) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (127 - 0)) + 0)
		sli_vibIntensity := real_to_int((((int_to_real(CC[101]) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (127 - 0)) + 0)
		call update.cc_vibrato()
	end if
end on

on note
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE, 1)
	ignore_event(EVENT_ID)
	release_note := - 1
	event_note := EVENT_NOTE
	event_velocity := EVENT_VELOCITY
	call update.lfoFreq()
	if(in_range(event_note, range[0], range[1]))
		if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
			iii := 0
			while(iii <= (NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
				get_sus_zone_ids(atk_sus_group, iii)
				set_control_par_str(lbl_sus_filename[iii], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_sample(sus_zone_ids[iii], NI_FILE_NAME))
				inc(iii)
			end while
		end if
		legato(EVENT_NOTE, title_groups, NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER, NUM_ATK_GROUPS, NUM_TRANS_GROUPS, btn_sustainFX)
	end if
	event_notes[event_note] := event_note
end on

on release
	release_note := EVENT_NOTE
	release_id := EVENT_ID
	release_notes()
	set_key_pressed(EVENT_NOTE, 0)
end on

on ui_control(mnu_rr)
	update.mnu_rr(play_velo, blip_note)
	call update.waveform()
end on

on ui_control(btn_play)
	call play_trans_sample()
end on

on ui_control(btn_reset)
	btn_reset := FALSE
	reset.label_texts()
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(check_button_state) - 1)) 
		set_control_par(check_button_state[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, TRUE)
		inc(i)
	end while
	btn_check_markSample := FALSE
	visibility.forallWindow(FALSE)
	visibility.resetWindow(TRUE)
end on

	btn_cancel := FALSE
	visibility.resetWindow(FALSE)
end on

on ui_control(btn_ok)
	btn_ok := FALSE
	call reset.arrays()
	save.arrays()
	visibility.resetWindow(FALSE)
	call init.arrays()
	call update.waveform()
end on

		i := 0
		while(i <= (num_elements(check_button_state) - 1)) 
			set_control_par(check_button_state[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, FALSE)
			inc(i)
		end while
		btn_check_releaseSus := TRUE
	else
		if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_check_releaseSus), CONTROL_PAR_KEY_SHIFT) = TRUE)
			i := 0
			while(i <= (num_elements(check_button_state) - 1)) 
				set_control_par(check_button_state[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, TRUE)
				inc(i)
			end while
		end if
	end if
end on

	btn_forall := FALSE
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(check_button_state) - 1)) 
		set_control_par(check_button_state[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, TRUE)
		inc(i)
	end while
	call update.zoneVolume()
	call update.sampleStart()
	call update.waitSus()
	call update.fadeInSus()
	call update.releaseSus()
	call update.fadeInTrans()
	call update.fadeOutTrans()
	visibility.resetWindow(FALSE)
	visibility.forallWindow(TRUE)
end on

on ui_control(btn_export_marked)
	btn_export_marked := FALSE
	scan.samples()
	i := 0
	while(i <= (2000 - 1)) 
		samples_to_revisit[i] := ""
		inc(i)
	end while
	ii := 0
	i := 0
	while(i <= (2000 - 1)) 
		if(marked_samples[i] = TRUE)
			samples_to_revisit[ii] := trans_file_names[i] & "     ->     " & intervals[i] & "     ->     " & sample_comments[i]
			inc(ii)
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	save_array_str(samples_to_revisit, data_path & "samples_to_revisit.nka")
end on

	all_windows.show(FALSE)
	btn_legatoSettings := TRUE
	legatoSettings.show(btn_legatoSettings)

on ui_control(btn_analyze)
	atk_sus_group := (title_groups + NUM_ATK_GROUPS) + title_groups
	message("atk_sus_group: " & atk_sus_group)
	get_keyrange(atk_sus_group)
	call update.keycolor()
	load.arrays()
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_loadedData), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legato_prefixes[prefix_idx])
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(txt_loadedData), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legato_prefixes[prefix_idx])
	iii := 0
	while(iii <= (NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
		get_sus_zone_ids(atk_sus_group, iii)
		set_control_par_str(lbl_sus_filename[iii], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_sample(sus_zone_ids[iii], NI_FILE_NAME))
		inc(iii)
	end while
	scan.samples()
	call update.waveform()
	call update.legatoArrays()
	update.legatoList()
	btn_analyze := FALSE
end on

	end if

		set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_volume), CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, 1)
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_volume), "Zone Vol.")
		save.arrays()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_prev)
	btn_prev := FALSE
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 0
	set_control_par(btn_element_button[element.idx - scroll.up], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + (element.idx - scroll.up)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + (element.idx - scroll.up)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + (element.idx - scroll.up)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
	if(element.idx # - 1)
		element.idx := legatoList.element_numbers[((element.idx - 1) + NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) mod NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS]
	else
		element.idx := legatoList.element_numbers[element.idx - 1]
	end if
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 1
	if((element.idx - scroll.up) = - 1)
		set_control_par(btn_element_button[(element.idx - scroll.up) + 1], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) + 1)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) + 1)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) + 1)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
	else
		set_control_par(btn_element_button[(element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - (12 - 1)) .and. sh_right((12 - 1) - (element.idx - scroll.up), 31))], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - (12 - 1)) .and. sh_right((12 - 1) - (element.idx - scroll.up), 31)))], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - (12 - 1)) .and. sh_right((12 - 1) - (element.idx - scroll.up), 31)))], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - (12 - 1)) .and. sh_right((12 - 1) - (element.idx - scroll.up), 31)))], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
	end if
	if(not in_range(element.idx, scroll.up, (scroll.up + 12) - 1))
		dec(scroll.up)
		call update.preset_button_focus()
		call update.scrollbar()
		call update.scrollarea()
	end if
	call load.element()
	if(btn_mute = TRUE)
		call play_trans_sample()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_next)
	btn_next := FALSE
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 0
	set_control_par(btn_element_button[element.idx - scroll.up], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 0)
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + (element.idx - scroll.up)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + (element.idx - scroll.up)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + (element.idx - scroll.up)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
	if(element.idx # - 1)
		element.idx := legatoList.element_numbers[(element.idx + 1) mod NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS]
	else
		element.idx := legatoList.element_numbers[0]
	end if
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 1
	if((element.idx - scroll.up) >= 12)
		set_control_par(btn_element_button[(element.idx - scroll.up) - 1], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - 1)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - 1)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - 1)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
	else
		set_control_par(btn_element_button[(element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0) .and. sh_right((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0, 31))], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, 1)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0) .and. sh_right((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0, 31)))], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0) .and. sh_right((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0, 31)))], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + ((element.idx - scroll.up) - (((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0) .and. sh_right((element.idx - scroll.up) - 0, 31)))], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
	end if
	if(not in_range(element.idx, scroll.up, (scroll.up + 12) - 1))
		inc(scroll.up)
		if(scroll.up > element.idx)
			scroll.up := element.idx
		else
			if((element.idx - scroll.up) > 12)
				scroll.up := (element.idx - 12) + 2
			end if
		end if
		call update.scrollbar()
		call update.scrollarea()
	end if
	call load.element()
	if(btn_mute = TRUE)
		call play_trans_sample()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(sli_scrollbar)
	if(NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
		scroll.up := (NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - (((NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) * sli_scrollbar) / 1000000)
		scroll.up := scroll.up
		scroll.realup := int_to_real(scroll.up)
		call update.scrollarea()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_element_completed0)
	completed_elements[legatoList.element_numbers[0 + scroll.up]] := get_control_par(btn_element_completed0, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	save.completed_array()
	call update.gui.legato()
end on

on ui_control(btn_element_marked0)
	legatoList.marked_elements[legatoList.element_numbers[0 + scroll.up]] := get_control_par(btn_element_marked0, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	set_control_par(txt_element_marked[0], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[get_control_par(btn_element_marked0, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
	set_control_par_str(txt_element_marked[0], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Comment and hit [Enter]")
	get_trans_idx_from_element(trans_idx, 0 + scroll.up)
	trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := legatoList.trans_zone_ids[0 + scroll.up]
	marked_samples[trans_idx] := get_control_par(btn_element_marked0, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	save.arrays()
	call update.gui.legato()
end on

on ui_control(btn_element_played0)
	btn_element_played0 := FALSE
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 0
	element.idx := 0 + scroll.up
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 1
	call update.scrollbar()
	call update.scrollarea()
	call load.element()
	call play_trans_sample()
	save.arrays()
end on

	call update.gui.legato()
end on

on ui_control(btn_element_played11)
	btn_element_played11 := FALSE
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 0
	element.idx := 11 + scroll.up
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 1
	call update.scrollbar()
	call update.scrollarea()
	call load.element()
	call play_trans_sample()
	save.arrays()
end on

on ui_control(txt_element_marked11)
	legatoList.comments[11 + scroll.up] := get_control_par_str(txt_element_marked11, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
	get_trans_idx_from_element(trans_idx, 11 + scroll.up)
	trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := legatoList.trans_zone_ids[11 + scroll.up]
	sample_comments[trans_idx] := get_control_par_str(txt_element_marked11, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT)
	save.arrays()
	call update.gui.legato()
end on

on ui_control(btn_element_button0)
	doubleclick_start(btn_element_button0, btn_listBrowserDC)
	if((element.idx # - 1) and (legatoList.element_numbers[element.idx] = legatoList.element_numbers[scroll.up + 0]))
		btn_element_button0 := TRUE
	else
		btn_elements_onoff[scroll.up + 0] := get_control_par(btn_element_button0, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	end if
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + 0], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + 0], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + 0], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button0 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(txt_element_marked[0], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button0 * 2) + 0])
	i := 0
	while(i <= (12 - 1)) 
		if(i # 0)
			set_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, FALSE)
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
			set_control_par(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 1)) 
		if(i # (scroll.up + 0))
			btn_elements_onoff[i] := 0
		else
			if(get_control_par(btn_element_button0, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = TRUE)
				element.idx := legatoList.element_numbers[i]
			else
				element.idx := - 1
			end if
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	call load.element()
	if(btn_mute = TRUE)
		call play_trans_sample()
	end if
	save.arrays()
	doubleclick_check(btn_listBrowserDC)
end on

		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	call load.element()
	if(btn_mute = TRUE)
		call play_trans_sample()
	end if
	save.arrays()
	doubleclick_check(btn_listBrowserDC)
end on

on ui_control(btn_element_button9)
	doubleclick_start(btn_element_button9, btn_listBrowserDC)
	if((element.idx # - 1) and (legatoList.element_numbers[element.idx] = legatoList.element_numbers[scroll.up + 9]))
		btn_element_button9 := TRUE
	else
		btn_elements_onoff[scroll.up + 9] := get_control_par(btn_element_button9, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
	end if
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + 9], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button9 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + 9], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button9 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + 9], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button9 * 2) + 0])
	set_control_par(txt_element_marked[9], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(btn_element_button9 * 2) + 0])
	i := 0
	while(i <= (12 - 1)) 
		if(i # 9)
			set_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, FALSE)
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
			set_control_par(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 1)) 
		if(i # (scroll.up + 9))
			btn_elements_onoff[i] := 0
		else
			if(get_control_par(btn_element_button9, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) = TRUE)
				element.idx := legatoList.element_numbers[i]
			else
				element.idx := - 1
			end if
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	call load.element()
	if(btn_mute = TRUE)
		call play_trans_sample()
	end if
	save.arrays()
	doubleclick_check(btn_listBrowserDC)
end on

on ui_control(sli_envRateCurve)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], get_ui_id(sli_envRateCurve), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.curve := sli_envRateCurve
	tbl_rate.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_rate.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_rate.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold := (((sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain := (((sli_envRateSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.decay) - ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_rate.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_rate.sustain
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.release) - ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.attack_idx := search(tbl_rate.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_rate.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[(((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_rate.curve < 500000)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i - (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_rate.release_idx)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i - tbl_rate.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_rate1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_rate2[i] := tbl_rate1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateCurve), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1) & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[0])
	if(0 = 4)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateCurve), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (sli_envRateCurve / 10000) & " %")
	end if
	last_time_envRateCurve := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_envRateCurve) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateCurve), envRateNames[0])
	end if
end on

on ui_control(sli_envRateAttack)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[1], get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.curve := sli_envRateCurve
	tbl_rate.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_rate.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_rate.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold := (((sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain := (((sli_envRateSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.decay) - ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_rate.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_rate.sustain
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.release) - ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.attack_idx := search(tbl_rate.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_rate.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[(((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_rate.curve < 500000)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i - (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_rate.release_idx)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i - tbl_rate.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_rate1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_rate2[i] := tbl_rate1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateAttack), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[1], vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1) & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[1])
	if(1 = 4)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateAttack), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (sli_envRateAttack / 10000) & " %")
	end if
	last_time_envRateAttack := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_envRateAttack) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateAttack), envRateNames[1])
	end if
end on

on ui_control(sli_envRateHold)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], get_ui_id(sli_envRateHold), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.curve := sli_envRateCurve
	tbl_rate.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_rate.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_rate.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold := (((sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain := (((sli_envRateSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.decay) - ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_rate.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_rate.sustain
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.release) - ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.attack_idx := search(tbl_rate.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_rate.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[(((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_rate.curve < 500000)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i - (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_rate.release_idx)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i - tbl_rate.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_rate1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_rate2[i] := tbl_rate1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateHold), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1) & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[2])
	if(2 = 4)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateHold), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (sli_envRateHold / 10000) & " %")
	end if
	last_time_envRateHold := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_envRateHold) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateHold), envRateNames[2])
	end if
end on

			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i - (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_rate.release_idx)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i - tbl_rate.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_rate1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_rate2[i] := tbl_rate1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateSustain), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[4], vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1) & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[4])
	if(4 = 4)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateSustain), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (sli_envRateSustain / 10000) & " %")
	end if
	last_time_envRateSustain := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_envRateSustain) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_envRateSustain), envRateNames[4])
	end if
end on

on ui_control(sli_rateEnv)
	call update.rateEnv()
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_rateEnv), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (int_to_real(sli_rateEnv / 1000) / 10) & " %")
	last_time_rateEnv := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_rateEnv) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_rateEnv), "Rate Envelope")
	end if
end on

on ui_control(sli_envIntCurve)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], get_ui_id(sli_envIntCurve), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.curve := sli_envIntCurve
	tbl_int.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_int.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_int.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_int.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_int.hold := (((sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_int.sustain := (((sli_envIntSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_int.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.decay) - ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_int.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_int.sustain
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.release) - ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.attack_idx := search(tbl_int.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_int.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[(((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold))
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.decayCurve[i - (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_int.release_idx)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i - tbl_int.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_int1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_int2[i] := tbl_int1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envIntCurve), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1) & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[0])
	if(0 = 4)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envIntCurve), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (sli_envIntCurve / 10000) & " %")
	end if
	last_time_envIntCurve := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_envIntCurve) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_envIntCurve), envRateNames[0])
	end if
end on

		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.decay) - ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_int.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_int.sustain
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.release) - ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.attack_idx := search(tbl_int.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_int.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[(((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold))
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.decayCurve[i - (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_int.release_idx)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i - tbl_int.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_int1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_int2[i] := tbl_int1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envIntHold), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, get_engine_par_disp(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[2], vibrato_groups[0], find_mod(vibrato_groups[0], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1) & " " & ADHSR_UNITS[2])
	if(2 = 4)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_envIntHold), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (sli_envIntHold / 10000) & " %")
	end if
	last_time_envIntHold := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_envIntHold) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_envIntHold), envRateNames[2])
	end if
end on

on ui_control(sli_envIntDecay)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[3], get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.curve := sli_envIntCurve
	tbl_int.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_int.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_int.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_int.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_int.hold := (((sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_int.sustain := (((sli_envIntSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_int.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.decay) - ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))

		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_int.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_int.sustain
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.release) - ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.attack_idx := search(tbl_int.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)

		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))

		inc(i)

	end if

on ui_control(sli_intEnv)
	call update.intEnv()
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_intEnv), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (int_to_real(sli_intEnv / 1000) / 10) & " %")
	last_time_intEnv := ENGINE_UPTIME
	wait(800 * 1000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - last_time_intEnv) > (800 - 5))
		set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_intEnv), "Intensity Envelope")
	end if
end on

end on

on ui_control(btn_prevPreset)
	btn_prevPreset := FALSE
	mnu_preset := ((mnu_preset - 1) + presetCount) mod presetCount
	call update.preset.menu()
	if(presetCount # 0)
		load.preset()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_nextPreset)
	btn_nextPreset := FALSE
	mnu_preset := (mnu_preset + 1) mod presetCount
	call update.preset.menu()
	if(presetCount # 0)
		load.preset()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_savePreset)
	btn_savePreset := FALSE
	save.preset()
end on

on ui_control(btn_deletePreset)
	btn_deletePreset := FALSE
	delete.preset()
end on

on ui_control(mouse_nka)
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DROP)
		wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset, NI_DND_ITEMS_ARRAY[0]))
		call load.array()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_scanPresets)
	if(preset_scan = FALSE)
		preset_scan := TRUE
		i := 0
		while(i <= (num_elements(vibPresetCount) - 1)) 
			vibPresetCount[i] := 0
			vibPresetNames[i] := ""
			inc(i)
		end while
		array.clear(vibrato_preset2)
		array.clear(vibrato_preset)
		presetCount := 0
		fs_navigate(get_ui_id(file_browser), 1)
	end if
end on

on ui_control(file_browser)
	message("File Browser triggered")
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser), 2)))
	if((preset_scan = TRUE) and (vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] # - 420))
		if(vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] = 0)
			if(not array_equal(vibrato_preset, vibrato_preset2))
				vibPresetNames[presetCount] := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser), 0)
				vibPresetCount[presetCount] := 1
				inc(presetCount)
			end if
			array.clear(vibrato_preset)
		else
			if(((vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] = 0) or (vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] = 1)) and (get_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets), CONTROL_PAR_KEY_ALT) = TRUE))
				message("Scanning for deleted")
				if(not array_equal(vibrato_preset, vibrato_preset2))
					vibPresetNames[presetCount] := fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser), 0)
					vibPresetCount[presetCount] := 1
					inc(presetCount)
					vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] := FALSE
					save_array_str(vibrato_preset, fs_get_filename(get_ui_id(file_browser), 2))
				end if
				array.clear(vibrato_preset)
			end if
		end if
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets), CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, TRUE)
		fs_navigate(get_ui_id(file_browser), 1)
	else
		message("The end")
		save.resource_arrays()
		get.presetCount()
		preset_scan := FALSE
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets), CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, FALSE)
		update.preset.menu()
		load.preset()
	end if
end on

on ui_control(mnu_preset)
	call update.preset.menu()
	load.preset()
end on

on async_complete
	if(NI_ASYNC_ID = save_id)
		if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = TRUE)
			save_id := - 1
		else
			if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = FALSE)
				save_id := 0
			end if
		end if
	end if
	if(NI_ASYNC_ID = load_id)
		if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = TRUE)
			load_id := - 1
		else
			if(NI_ASYNC_EXIT_STATUS = FALSE)
				load_id := 0
			end if
		end if
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_home)
	all_windows.show(FALSE)
	btn_home := TRUE
	home.show(btn_home)
end on

end on

end on
