function load.array() : Unknown
	i := preset_idx.BODY
	while(i <= (100 - 1)) 
		if(uiControls[i - preset_idx.BODY] # 0)
			set_control_par(uiControls[i - preset_idx.BODY], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, vibrato_preset[i])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[0], get_ui_id(sli_envRateCurve), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.curve := sli_envRateCurve
	tbl_rate.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_rate.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_rate.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold := (((sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain := (((sli_envRateSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.decay) - ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_rate.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_rate.sustain
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.release) - ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.attack_idx := search(tbl_rate.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_rate.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[(((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_rate.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_rate.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_rate.curve < 500000)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_rate.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_rate.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_rate.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_rate.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_rate.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold))
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i - (tbl_rate.attack_idx + tbl_rate.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[tbl_rate.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_rate.release_idx)
			tbl_rate.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i - tbl_rate.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_rate1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_rate.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_rate2[i] := tbl_rate1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[1], get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_rate.curve := sli_envRateCurve
	tbl_rate.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_rate.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_rate.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_rate.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_rate.hold := (((sli_envRateHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_rate.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envRateDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_rate.sustain := (((sli_envRateSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_rate.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_rate.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_rate.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_rate.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.decay) - ((((tbl_rate.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_rate.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_rate.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_rate.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_rate.sustain
		tbl_rate.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_rate.release) - ((((tbl_rate.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))

	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else

		end if
		if(i > (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold))
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.decayCurve[i - (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1))

			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i - tbl_int.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_int1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_int2[i] := tbl_int1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[3], get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.curve := sli_envIntCurve
	tbl_int.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_int.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_int.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_int.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_int.hold := (((sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_int.sustain := (((sli_envIntSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_int.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.decay) - ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_int.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_int.sustain
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.release) - ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.attack_idx := search(tbl_int.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_int.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[(((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold))
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.decayCurve[i - (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_int.release_idx)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i - tbl_int.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1)) 
		tbl_int1[i] := ((((((real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]) - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[i]), 31))) - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(1000) * 0.88) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		tbl_int2[i] := tbl_int1[i]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ADHSR_ENGINE_PARAMS[4], get_ui_id(sli_envIntSustain), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.curve := sli_envIntCurve
	tbl_int.attack_point := pow(10, (log(1.5) / log(10)) + ((((int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.51) - 0) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) - 0)) * ((log(0.056) / log(10)) - (log(1.5) / log(10)))))
	tbl_int.release_idx := real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.75)
	tbl_int.attack := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntAttack)) - 0) * (tbl_int.attack_point - 1.5)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 1.5
	tbl_int.hold := (((sli_envIntHold - 0) * (real_to_int(int_to_real(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS) * 0.15) - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.decay := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_envIntDecay)) - 0) * (15000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	tbl_int.sustain := (((sli_envIntSustain - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0
	tbl_int.release := (((int_to_real(750000) - 0) * (40000 - 800)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 800
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := real_to_int(exp(tbl_int.attack * int_to_real(i)))
		tbl_int.expCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.expCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.expCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (11 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.decay) - ((((tbl_int.decay - 800) * (200 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.decayCurve[i], 31))
		tbl_int.decayCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.decayCurve[i] - 0) * (1000 - tbl_int.sustain)) / (1000 - 0)) + tbl_int.sustain
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := real_to_int(((1 / (int_to_real(i) + ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (5 - 0.01)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0.01))) * tbl_int.release) - ((((tbl_int.release - 800) * (300 - 0)) / (15000 - 800)) + 0))
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := ((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] * (1 + (sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0, 31))) - (1000 * sh_right(1000 - tbl_int.releaseCurve[i], 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
	tbl_int.attack_idx := search(tbl_int.expCurve, 1000)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.linCurve[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(i) - 0) * (int_to_real(1000) - 0)) / (int_to_real(tbl_int.attack_idx) - 0)) + 0)
		tbl_int.logCurve[i] := 1000 - tbl_int.expCurve[(((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) * (1 + (sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31) .or. sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((tbl_int.attack_idx - i) - 0, 31))) - (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS * sh_right(tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - (tbl_int.attack_idx - i), 31))]
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(tbl_int.curve < 500000)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.expCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (0 - 1)) / (500000 - 0)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 0, 31))) - (500000 * sh_right(500000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 0) * (1 - 0)) / (500000 - 0)) + 0))
		else
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := (int_to_real(tbl_int.linCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (0 - 1)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 1)) + (int_to_real(tbl_int.logCurve[i]) * ((((int_to_real(((tbl_int.curve * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31) .or. sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31)))) - (500000 * sh_right(tbl_int.curve - 500000, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - tbl_int.curve, 31))) - 500000) * (1 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 500000)) + 0))
		end if
		if(i > (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold))
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.decayCurve[i - (tbl_int.attack_idx + tbl_int.hold)])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] := (((tbl_int.releaseCurve[i] - 0) * (real_to_int(tbl_int.env_array[tbl_int.release_idx]) - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(tbl_int.env_array) - 1)) 
		if(i > tbl_int.release_idx)
			tbl_int.env_array[i] := int_to_real(tbl_int.releaseCurve[i - tbl_int.release_idx])
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while

	while(i <= (tbl_int.NUM_TABLE_STEPS - 1))

	call update.intEnv()
	call update.gainModulation()
	call update.pitchModulation()
	call update.lfoFreq()
	call update.lfoRand()
	call update.lfoFadeIn()
	call update.eqFreq()
	call update.eqBandwidth()
	call update.eqGain()
	call update.vibIntensity()
end function

function save.preset() : Unknown
	load_id := load_array_str(vibrato_preset, base_path & txt_presetName & ".nka")
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset, base_path & txt_presetName & ".nka"))
	if(load_id # - 1)
		vibPresetCount[presetCount] := 1
		vibPresetNames[presetCount] := txt_presetName
		save.resource_arrays()
		mnu_preset := presetCount
		presetCount := (((presetCount + 1) * (1 + (sh_right(100 - (presetCount + 1), 31) .or. sh_right((presetCount + 1) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((presetCount + 1) - 0, 31))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - (presetCount + 1), 31))
		preset_scan := TRUE
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_scanPresets), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE, "alpha")
	end if
	vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] := FALSE
	i := preset_idx.BODY
	while(i <= (100 - 1)) 
		if(uiControls[i - preset_idx.BODY] # 0)
			vibrato_preset[i] := get_control_par(uiControls[i - preset_idx.BODY], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	save_array_str(vibrato_preset, base_path & txt_presetName & ".nka")
	call update.preset.menu()
end function

function load.resource_arrays() : Unknown
	load_array(vibPresetCount, 1)
	load_array(vibPresetNames, 1)
end function

function update.lfoFadeIn() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_LFO_DELAY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_lfoFadeIn)) - 0) * (900000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.lfoFreq() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_INTMOD_FREQUENCY, real_to_int((((int_to_real((((sli_lfoFreq + lfoRandValues[event_note]) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - (sli_lfoFreq + lfoRandValues[event_note]), 31) .or. sh_right((sli_lfoFreq + lfoRandValues[event_note]) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((sli_lfoFreq + lfoRandValues[event_note]) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - (sli_lfoFreq + lfoRandValues[event_note]), 31))) - 0) * (650000 - 450000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 450000), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.pitchModulation() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_pitchModulation)) - 0) * (200000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_PITCH"))
		inc(i)
	end while
	current_pitchModulation := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_pitchModulation)) - 0) * (200000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0)
end function

function update.cc_vibrato() : Unknown
	set_controller(101, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_vibrato)) - 0) * (127 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0))
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, get_ui_id(sli_vibrato), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_EQ_GAIN_1"))
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, (((sli_vibrato - 0) * (current_pitchModulation - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0, vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), find_target(vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), "LFO_MULTI D" & "_PITCH"))
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function vibrato.show(Boolean : int) : Unknown
	btn_vibratoSettings := Boolean
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_vibrato), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
end function

function doubleclick_start(uiControl : any, doubleclickControl : int) : Unknown
	set_control_par(doubleclickControl, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, get_control_par(uiControl, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X))
	set_control_par(doubleclickControl, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(uiControl, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y))
	set_control_par(doubleclickControl, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, get_control_par(uiControl, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH))
	set_control_par(doubleclickControl, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, get_control_par(uiControl, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT))
	set_control_par(doubleclickControl, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
	doubleclickControl := FALSE
	clicktime[0] := get_ui_id(uiControl)
	clicktime[1] := ENGINE_UPTIME
end function

function update.preset_button_focus() : Unknown
	if(element.idx # - 1)
		btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 1
		if(not in_range(element.idx, scroll.up, scroll.up + 12))
			scroll.up := element.idx - ((12 - 1) / 2)
		end if
		if((element.idx - 2) <= scroll.up)
			scroll.up := element.idx - 2
		else
			if((element.idx + 2) > ((scroll.up + 12) - 1))
				scroll.up := (element.idx + 2) - (12 - 1)
			end if
		end if
		scroll.up := (scroll.up * (1 + (sh_right((NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - scroll.up, 31) .or. sh_right(scroll.up - 0, 31)))) - ((NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) * sh_right((NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - scroll.up, 31))
	end if
end function

function load.element() : Unknown
	if(1 = TRUE)
		play_event := lsb(legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element.idx])
		play_velo := msb(legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element.idx])
	else
		play_event := get_zone_par(legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element.idx], ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
		play_velo := get_zone_par(legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element.idx], ZONE_PAR_LOW_VELO)
	end if
	current_trans_group := trans_group + legatoList.trans_zone_groups[element.idx]
	mnu_rr := legatoList.trans_zone_groups[element.idx]
	transition_id := play_note(play_event, play_velo, 0, - 1)
	change_vol(transition_id, - 200000, 0)
	set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
	set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, current_trans_group)
	wait(1)
	get_trans_idx(trans_idx, transition_id)
	attach_zone(get_ui_id(wf_transition), get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
	trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element.idx]
	trans_zone_volume[trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
	trans_zone_pan[trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_PAN)
	trans_file_names[trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), NI_FILE_NAME)
	note_off(transition_id)
	call update.gui.legato()
	call update.gui.sustain()
	call reset.label_texts()
	update.interval_keycolor(played_interval[0], played_interval[1])
end function

function get_element_idx_from_trans(result : int, trans_idx : Unknown) : int
	btn_elements_onoff[0 - ((0 - element.idx) .and. sh_right(0 - element.idx, 31))] := 0
	result := 0 - ((0 - search(legatoList.trans_zone_ids, trans_zone_ids[trans_idx])) .and. sh_right(0 - search(legatoList.trans_zone_ids, trans_zone_ids[trans_idx]), 31))
	btn_elements_onoff[element.idx] := 1
end function

function update.scrollbar() : Unknown
	sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / (NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * scroll.up)
end function

function update.scrollarea() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (12 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(btn_element_completed[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(btn_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(btn_element_played[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
		set_control_par_str(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legatoList.trans_file_names[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par_str(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legatoList.trans_zone_ids[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par_str(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legatoList.intervals[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par_str(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, legatoList.comments[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, btn_elements_onoff[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(get_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE) * 2) + 0])
		set_control_par(btn_element_completed[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, completed_elements[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par(btn_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, legatoList.marked_elements[i + scroll.up])
		set_control_par(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[legatoList.marked_elements[i + scroll.up]])
		if(legatoList.end_of_list[i + scroll.up] = - 1)
			set_control_par(btn_element_button[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(2 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(3 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(_lbl_file_infos[(5 * 12) + i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(btn_element_completed[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(btn_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(btn_element_played[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
			set_control_par(txt_element_marked[i], CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scrollhandle), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_scrollbar), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - handle_size) - ((sli_scrollbar * (245 - handle_size)) / 1000000)))
end function

function load.preset() : Unknown
	wait_async(load_array_str(vibrato_preset, base_path & vibPresetNames[mnu_preset] & ".nka"))
	call load.array()
end function

function get.presetCount() : Unknown
	presetCount := search(vibPresetCount, 0)
	presetCount := ((presetCount * (1 + (sh_right(100 - presetCount, 31) .or. sh_right(presetCount - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(presetCount - 0, 31))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - presetCount, 31))
end function

function update.eqGain() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_GAIN1, get_ui_id(sli_eqGain), vibrato_groups[i], 5, 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function accum(array_variable : int[], array_result : int[]) : Unknown
	declare hold : int := 0
	i := 0
	while(i <= (7 - 1)) 
		ii := 0
		while(ii <= i) 
			hold := (hold + array_variable[ii]) + 9
			inc(ii)
		end while
		array_result[i + 1] := hold
		hold := 0
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.gainModulation() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_LFO_SINE, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_gainModulation)) - 0) * (1e+06 - 500000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 500000), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "LFO_MULTI D"), - 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function save.completed_array() : Unknown
	save_array_str(completed_elements, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "completed_elements.nka")
end function

function update.releaseSus() : Unknown
	declare zw : real := 0
	sus_release_time[trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseSus), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, sus_release_time[trans_idx] & " ms")
	zw := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((zw * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((zw * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((zw * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((zw * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((zw * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31)))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (99 - 0)) + 0))
end function

function update.fadeOutTrans() : Unknown
	trans_fadeOut_time[trans_idx] := sli_fadeOutTrans
	current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeOutTrans)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutTrans), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int(current_fadeInTime) & " ms")
	real := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeOutTrans)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutCurve), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31)))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (99 - 0)) + 0))
end function

function update.sampleStart() : Unknown
	declare cursor_scale : int
	slider := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_samplestart)) - 0) * (int_to_real(max_samplestart * 1000) - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0)
	trans_zone_start[trans_idx] := ((real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000) * (1 + (sh_right(sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000) - 0, 31))) - (sample_end * sh_right(sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000), 31))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, real_to_int((((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx]) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_end) - 0)) + 0))
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestart), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ((((sli_samplestart - 0) * (max_samplestart - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0) & " ms")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (99 - 0)) + 0))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (99 - 0)) + 0))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (99 - 0)) + 0))
	current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeInSus)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31)))
	current_waitTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_waitSus)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 2) + real_to_int(((((current_waitTime * 1000) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, (555 - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X)) - 2)
end function

		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(txt_sampleComment), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Leave a comment and hit [Enter]")
	else
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(txt_sampleComment), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, sample_comments[trans_idx])
	end if
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(txt_sampleComment), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_markSample])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_sampleCommentBG), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_markSample])
end function

	development[0] := - 1
	_id := load_array_str(development, development_path)
	if(_id = - 1)
	end if
end function

function Rand(result : int, min : number, max : number) : int
	___M.Seed := (8088405 * ___M.Seed) + 1
	result := ((sh_right(___M.Seed, 8) .and. 16777215) mod ((max - min) + 1)) + min
end function

function settings.show(Boolean : int) : Unknown
	btn_settings := Boolean
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_settings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
end function

function update.legatoList() : Unknown
	declare z : int
	NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD := NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS
	NUM_PRESETS := search(zone_ids_master, - 1)
	NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS := NUM_PRESETS
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_presetcount), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS & "/" & NUM_PRESETS)
	if(NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD # NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
		z := 0
		while(z <= (num_elements(legatoList.end_of_list) - 1)) 
			legatoList.end_of_list[z] := - 1
			if(z < NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS)
				legatoList.end_of_list[z] := 1
			end if
			inc(z)
		end while
	end if
	scroll.up := real_to_int((((scroll.realup - 0) * (int_to_real(NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12) - 0)) / (int_to_real(NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS_OLD - 12) - 0)) + 0)
	update.preset_button_focus()
	update.scrollbar()
	update.scrollarea()
	if(NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS > 12)
		sli_scrollbar := 1000000 - ((1000000 / (NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS - 12)) * scroll.up)
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_scrollbar), CONTROL_PAR_MOUSE_BEHAVIOUR, - ((((422 - 245) * 12) * 2) + (2 * (NUM_PRESETS - NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS))))
		handle_size := real_to_int(round(int_to_real(245) / (int_to_real(NUM_SHOWN_PRESETS) / int_to_real(12))))
		if(handle_size < 30)
			handle_size := 30
		end if
	else
		sli_scrollbar := 1000000
		handle_size := 245
	end if
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scrollhandle), CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT, handle_size)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scrollhandle), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y, get_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_scrollbar), CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y) + ((245 - handle_size) - ((sli_scrollbar * (245 - handle_size)) / 1000000)))
end function

function update.lfoRand() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(lfoRandValues) - 1)) 
		lfoRandValues[i] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(randNoteValues[i]) - - 500) * (int_to_real(sli_lfoRand / 10) - - int_to_real(sli_lfoRand / 10))) / (500 - - 500)) + - int_to_real(sli_lfoRand / 10))
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function doubleclick_check(doubleclickControl : Unknown) : Unknown
	wait((CLICK_INTERVAL * 1000) + 2000)
	if((ENGINE_UPTIME - clicktime[1]) > CLICK_INTERVAL)
		set_control_par(doubleclickControl, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
		clicktime[2] := FALSE
	end if
end function

function update.intEnv() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_intEnv)) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), find_target(vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR2"), "ENV_AHDSR2" & "_INTENSITY"))
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.preset.menu() : Unknown
	if(presetCount = 0)
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(txt_presetName), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "EMPTY PRESET")
	else
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(txt_presetName), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, vibPresetNames[get_control_par(get_ui_id(mnu_preset), CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)])
	end if
	i := 0
	while(i <= (100 - 1)) 
		if(i < presetCount)
			set_menu_item_str(get_ui_id(mnu_preset), i, vibPresetNames[i])
			set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id(mnu_preset), i, TRUE)
		else
			set_menu_item_visibility(get_ui_id(mnu_preset), i, FALSE)
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function array.clear(array : int[]) : Unknown
	lib.i := 0
	while(lib.i <= (num_elements(array) - 1)) 
		array[lib.i] := 0
		inc(lib.i)
	end while
end function

function visibility.resetWindow(Boolean : Unknown) : Unknown
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_reset), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs(Boolean) - 1, 31))])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_resetWindow), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_checkButtons), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
end function
