	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_FREQ1, get_ui_id(sli_eqFreq), vibrato_groups[i], 5, 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.fadeInSus() : Unknown
	sus_fadeIn_time[trans_idx] := sli_fadeInSus
	current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeInSus)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInSus), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int(current_fadeInTime) & " ms")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31)))
end function

function home.show(Boolean : int) : Unknown
	btn_home := Boolean
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_home), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_reverb), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_eq), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
end function

function update.gui.sustain() : Unknown
	sli_releaseSus := real_to_int((((int_to_real(sus_release_time[trans_idx]) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (1000 - 0)) + 0)
	call update.releaseSus()
	sli_waitSus := trans_wait_time[trans_idx]
	call update.waitSus()
	sli_fadeInSus := sus_fadeIn_time[trans_idx]
	call update.fadeInSus()
end function

function update.fadeInTrans() : Unknown
	trans_fadeIn_time[trans_idx] := sli_fadeInTrans
	current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeInTrans)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInTrans), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int(current_fadeInTime) & " ms")
	real := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeInTrans)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInCurve), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((real * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31)))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, 2 + real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE)) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (99 - 0)) + 0))
end function

function update.rateEnv() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_MOD_TARGET_INTENSITY, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_rateEnv)) - 0) * (350000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0), vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), find_target(vibrato_groups[i], find_mod(vibrato_groups[i], "ENV_AHDSR"), "ENV_AHDSR" & "_FREQUENCY"))
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.waitSus() : Unknown
	trans_wait_time[trans_idx] := sli_waitSus
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_waitSus), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_waitSus)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0) & " ms")
	current_fadeInTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_fadeInSus)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, ((real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) * (1 + (sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0) - 0, 31))) - (99 * sh_right(99 - real_to_int(((((current_fadeInTime * 1000) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0), 31)))
	current_waitTime := (((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_waitSus)) - 0) * (500 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X, (get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X) + 2) + real_to_int(((((current_waitTime * 1000) - 0) * (int_to_real(555) - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_length) - 0)) + 0))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH, (555 - get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_POS_X)) - 2)
end function

function non_rpt_random(result : int, last_random : int, min_random : int, max_random : int) : int
	Rand(result, min_random + 1, max_random)
	result := (last_random + result) mod (max_random + 1)
	last_random := result
end function

function save.resource_arrays() : Unknown
	save_array(vibPresetNames, 1)
	save_array(vibPresetCount, 1)
end function

function load.arrays() : Unknown
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_file_names, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_file_names.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(intervals, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "intervals.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_zone_ids, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_ids.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_zone_start, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_start.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_event_volume, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_event_volume.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_wait_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_wait_time.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_fadeIn_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeIn_time.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(trans_fadeOut_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeOut_time.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(sus_release_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "sus_release_time.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(sus_fadeIn_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "sus_fadeIn_time.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(marked_samples, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "marked_samples.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(sample_comments, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "sample_comments.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(file_names_master, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "file_names_master.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(zone_ids_master, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "zone_ids_master.nka"))
	wait_async(load_array_str(completed_elements, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "completed_elements.nka"))
	init.arrays()
end function

function get_trans_idx(result : int, event_id : int) : int
	if(1 = TRUE)
		if(search(trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))) = - 1)
			result := search(trans_zone_ids, - 1)
		else
			result := search(trans_zone_ids, (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)))
		end if
	else
		if(search(trans_zone_ids, get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)) = - 1)
			result := search(trans_zone_ids, - 1)
		else
			result := search(trans_zone_ids, get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
		end if
	end if
end function

function reset.arrays() : Unknown
	declare accum : int := 0
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(check_button_state) - 1)) 
		accum := accum + get_control_par(check_button_state[i], CONTROL_PAR_VALUE)
		inc(i)
	end while
	i := 0
	while(i <= (2000 - 1)) 
		if(accum = num_elements(check_button_state))
			trans_file_names[i] := ""
			trans_zone_ids[i] := - 1
			file_names_master[i] := ""
			zone_ids_master[i] := - 1
			samples_to_revisit[i] := ""
			intervals[i] := ""
			sus_file_names[i] := ""
			sus_zone_ids[i] := - 1
			sus_zone_volume[i] := 0
		end if
		sus_release_time[i] := sus_release_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))
		trans_zone_start[i] := trans_zone_start[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))
		trans_event_volume[i] := trans_event_volume[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))
		trans_wait_time[i] := trans_wait_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))
		sus_fadeIn_time[i] := sus_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))
		trans_fadeIn_time[i] := trans_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))
		trans_fadeOut_time[i] := trans_fadeOut_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))
		marked_samples[i] := marked_samples[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_markSample) - 1, 31))
		if(btn_check_markSample = TRUE)
			sample_comments[i] := ""
		end if
		completed_elements[i] := completed_elements[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_completed) - 1, 31))
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function update.zoneVolume() : Unknown
	trans_event_volume[trans_idx] := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_volume), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, (int_to_real(real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000) / 10) / 100) & " dB")
end function

function update.cc_expression() : Unknown
	set_controller(111, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_expression)) - 0) * (127 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0))
end function

function apply.forall.settings() : Unknown
	slider := real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_samplestart)) - 0) * (int_to_real(max_samplestart * 1000) - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0)
	ii := ((real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000) * (1 + (sh_right(sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000), 31) .or. sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000) - 0, 31))) - (sample_end * sh_right(sample_end - real_to_int((int_to_real(slider) / 1e+06) * 48000), 31))
	i := 0
	while(i <= (2000 - 1)) 
		if(i # trans_idx)
			sus_release_time[i] := ((((sus_release_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0) * btn_check_releaseSus)) * (1 + (sh_right(real_to_int(1000) - ((sus_release_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0) * btn_check_releaseSus)), 31) .or. sh_right(((sus_release_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0) * btn_check_releaseSus)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((sus_release_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0) * btn_check_releaseSus)) - 0, 31))) - (real_to_int(1000) * sh_right(real_to_int(1000) - ((sus_release_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_releaseSus) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_releaseSus)) - 0) * (1000 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0) * btn_check_releaseSus)), 31))
			trans_zone_start[i] := ((((trans_zone_start[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + (ii * btn_check_samplestart)) * (1 + (sh_right(real_to_int(((int_to_real(max_samplestart) * 1000) / 1e+06) * 48000) - ((trans_zone_start[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + (ii * btn_check_samplestart)), 31) .or. sh_right(((trans_zone_start[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + (ii * btn_check_samplestart)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((trans_zone_start[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + (ii * btn_check_samplestart)) - 0, 31))) - (real_to_int(((int_to_real(max_samplestart) * 1000) / 1e+06) * 48000) * sh_right(real_to_int(((int_to_real(max_samplestart) * 1000) / 1e+06) * 48000) - ((trans_zone_start[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_samplestart) - 1, 31))) + (ii * btn_check_samplestart)), 31))
			trans_event_volume[i] := ((((trans_event_volume[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000) * btn_check_volume)) * (1 + (sh_right(10000 - ((trans_event_volume[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000) * btn_check_volume)), 31) .or. sh_right(((trans_event_volume[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000) * btn_check_volume)) - - 10000, 31)))) - (- 10000 * sh_right(((trans_event_volume[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000) * btn_check_volume)) - - 10000, 31))) - (10000 * sh_right(10000 - ((trans_event_volume[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_volume) - 1, 31))) + (real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_volume)) - 0) * (10000 - - 10000)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + - 10000) * btn_check_volume)), 31))
			trans_wait_time[i] := ((((trans_wait_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_waitSus * btn_check_waitSus)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((trans_wait_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_waitSus * btn_check_waitSus)), 31) .or. sh_right(((trans_wait_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_waitSus * btn_check_waitSus)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((trans_wait_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_waitSus * btn_check_waitSus)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((trans_wait_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_waitSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_waitSus * btn_check_waitSus)), 31))
			sus_fadeIn_time[i] := ((((sus_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInSus * btn_check_fadeInSus)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((sus_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInSus * btn_check_fadeInSus)), 31) .or. sh_right(((sus_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInSus * btn_check_fadeInSus)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((sus_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInSus * btn_check_fadeInSus)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((sus_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInSus) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInSus * btn_check_fadeInSus)), 31))
			trans_fadeIn_time[i] := ((((trans_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInTrans * btn_check_fadeInTrans)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((trans_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInTrans * btn_check_fadeInTrans)), 31) .or. sh_right(((trans_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInTrans * btn_check_fadeInTrans)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((trans_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInTrans * btn_check_fadeInTrans)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((trans_fadeIn_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeInTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeInTrans * btn_check_fadeInTrans)), 31))
			trans_fadeOut_time[i] := ((((trans_fadeOut_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeOutTrans * btn_check_fadeOutTrans)) * (1 + (sh_right(1000000 - ((trans_fadeOut_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeOutTrans * btn_check_fadeOutTrans)), 31) .or. sh_right(((trans_fadeOut_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeOutTrans * btn_check_fadeOutTrans)) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right(((trans_fadeOut_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeOutTrans * btn_check_fadeOutTrans)) - 0, 31))) - (1000000 * sh_right(1000000 - ((trans_fadeOut_time[i] * abs(sh_right(abs(btn_check_fadeOutTrans) - 1, 31))) + (sli_fadeOutTrans * btn_check_fadeOutTrans)), 31))
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function get_sus_zone_ids(base_group : number, iterator : number) : Unknown
	blip_note := play_note(event_note, 1, 1, - 1)
	change_vol(blip_note, - 200000, 0)
	set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
	set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, base_group + iterator)
	wait(1)
	sus_zone_ids[iterator] := get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
	fade_out(blip_note, 0, 1)
end function

function update.mnu_rr(event_velocity : number, note_id : Unknown) : Unknown
	if(mnu_rr = NUM_TRANS_GROUPS)
		i := 0
		while(i <= (NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
			if(in_range(event_velocity, _trans_ranges[(i * 2) + 0], _trans_ranges[(i * 2) + 1]))
				current_trans_group := trans_group + i
			end if
			inc(i)
		end while
	else
		if(mnu_rr = (NUM_TRANS_GROUPS + 1))
			_trans_rr[(get_event_par(note_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par(note_id, EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] := (_trans_rr[(get_event_par(note_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par(note_id, EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)] + 1) mod NUM_TRANS_GROUPS
			current_trans_group := trans_group + _trans_rr[(get_event_par(note_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE) * 24) + (get_event_par(note_id, EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY) / 5)]
		else
			current_trans_group := trans_group + mnu_rr
		end if
	end if
end function

function save.arrays() : Unknown
	async_ids[0] := save_array_str(trans_file_names, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_file_names.nka")
	async_ids[1] := save_array_str(intervals, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "intervals.nka")
	async_ids[2] := save_array_str(trans_zone_ids, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_ids.nka")
	async_ids[3] := save_array_str(trans_event_volume, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_event_volume.nka")
	async_ids[4] := save_array_str(trans_zone_start, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_zone_start.nka")
	async_ids[5] := save_array_str(trans_wait_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_wait_time.nka")
	async_ids[6] := save_array_str(sus_release_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "sus_release_time.nka")
	async_ids[7] := save_array_str(sus_fadeIn_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "sus_fadeIn_time.nka")
	async_ids[8] := save_array_str(marked_samples, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "marked_samples.nka")
	async_ids[9] := save_array_str(sample_comments, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "sample_comments.nka")
	async_ids[10] := save_array_str(trans_fadeIn_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeIn_time.nka")
	async_ids[11] := save_array_str(trans_fadeOut_time, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "trans_fadeOut_time.nka")
	async_ids[12] := save_array_str(completed_elements, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "completed_elements.nka")
end function

function play_trans_sample() : Unknown
	play_id := play_note(play_event, play_velo, real_to_int((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx]) / 48000) * 1e+06), - 1)
	set_event_par_arr(play_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
	set_event_par_arr(play_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, current_trans_group)
	set_event_par_arr(play_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, get_ui_id(sli_fadeInTrans), 3)
	set_event_par_arr(play_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, get_ui_id(sli_fadeOutTrans), 5)
	change_vol(play_id, trans_event_volume[trans_idx], 0)
end function

function visibility.forallWindow(Boolean : Unknown) : Unknown
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_forall), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[abs(sh_right(abs(Boolean) - 1, 31))])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_forallWindow), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_checkButtons), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[Boolean])
end function

function check_decoding() : Unknown
	decode[0] := - 1
	_id := load_array_str(decode, decode_path)
	if(_id = - 1)
	end if
end function

function update.waveform() : Unknown
	transition_id := play_note(play_event, play_velo, 0, - 1)
	change_vol(transition_id, - 200000, 0)
	set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
	update.mnu_rr(play_velo, transition_id)
	set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, current_trans_group)
	wait(1)
	get_trans_idx(trans_idx, transition_id)
	attach_zone(get_ui_id(wf_transition), get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
	get_element_idx_from_trans(element.idx, trans_idx)
	if(1 = TRUE)
		trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
	else
		trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
	end if
	trans_zone_volume[trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
	trans_zone_pan[trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_PAN)
	trans_file_names[trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), NI_FILE_NAME)
	fade_out(transition_id, 0, 1)
	call update.gui.legato()
	call update.gui.sustain()
	call reset.label_texts()
end function

function legato(note : number, start_group : int, num_dynamic_layers : int, num_rr : int, trans_groups : int, sustain_fx : int) : Unknown
	atk_group := start_group
	atk_sus_group := (atk_group + num_rr) + title_groups
	sus_group := (atk_sus_group + num_dynamic_layers) + title_groups
	sus_fx_group := (sus_group + num_dynamic_layers) + title_groups
	trans_group := (sus_fx_group + (num_dynamic_layers * sustain_fx)) + title_groups
	sus_rls_group := (trans_group + trans_groups) + title_groups
	message("atk_sus_group: " & atk_sus_group & ", sus_group: " & sus_group & ", trans_group: " & trans_group)
	num_notes := 0
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(KEY_DOWN) - 1)) 
		num_notes := KEY_DOWN[i] + num_notes
		inc(i)
	end while
	interval := EVENT_NOTE - last_note
	if(((num_notes > 1) and (note # last_note)) and (is_attack # - 1))
		is_attack := FALSE
		if(abs(interval) <= 12)
			if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
				update.interval_keycolor(note, note - interval)
			end if
			blip_note := play_note((note * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right(interval - 0, 31) + 1) - 1, 31))) + (last_note * (sh_right(interval - 0, 31) + 1)), (abs(interval) * 5) + ((sh_right(interval - 0, 31) + 1) * 60), 0, - 1)
			change_vol(blip_note, - 200000, 0)
			set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
			update.mnu_rr(EVENT_VELOCITY, blip_note)
			set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, current_trans_group)
			wait(1)
			get_trans_idx(trans_idx, blip_note)
			if(1 = TRUE)
				trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
			else
				trans_zone_ids[trans_idx] := get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
			end if
			fade_out(event_id, sus_release_time[trans_idx] * 1000, 1)
			fade_out(attack_id, 200000, 1)
			fade_out(last_transition, 200000, 1)
			fade_out(blip_note, 0, 1)
			transition_id := play_note((note * abs(sh_right(abs(sh_right(interval - 0, 31) + 1) - 1, 31))) + (last_note * (sh_right(interval - 0, 31) + 1)), (abs(interval) * 5) + ((sh_right(interval - 0, 31) + 1) * 60), real_to_int((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx]) / 48000) * 1e+06), 0)
			update.mnu_rr(EVENT_VELOCITY, transition_id)
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, trans_fadeIn_time[trans_idx], 3)
			set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, trans_fadeOut_time[trans_idx], 5)
			play_event := get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE)
			play_velo := get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_VELOCITY)
			if(btn_legato = TRUE)
				set_event_par_arr(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, current_trans_group)
				change_vol(transition_id, trans_event_volume[trans_idx], 0)
				if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
					wait(1)
					trans_zone_volume[trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_VOLUME)
					trans_zone_pan[trans_idx] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_PAN)
					trans_file_names[trans_idx] := get_sample(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), NI_FILE_NAME)
					attach_zone(get_ui_id(wf_transition), get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), 0)
					get_element_idx_from_trans(element.idx, trans_idx)
					if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_legatoList), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE) = HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
						call update.legatoList()
					end if
					call update.gui.legato()
					intervals[trans_idx] := playedInterval
				end if
			end if
			if(btn_sus = TRUE)
				event_id := play_note(note, EVENT_VELOCITY, sus_s_start, - 1)
				set_event_mark(event_id, MARK_1)
				sus_rr[note] := (sus_rr[note] + 1) mod 3
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, trans_wait_time[trans_idx], 0)
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, sus_fadeIn_time[trans_idx], 2)
				if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
					call update.gui.sustain()
				end if
			end if
			set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
			i := 0
			while(i <= (NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, i + sus_group)
				inc(i)
			end while
			i := 0
			while(i <= NUM_SUSTAIN_FX_GROUPS) 
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, i + sus_fx_group)
				inc(i)
			end while
		else
			fade_out(event_id, 152 * 1000, 1)
			event_id := play_note(note, EVENT_VELOCITY, sus_s_start, - 1)
			set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, 150000, 0)
			set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_MOD_VALUE_ID, DEFAULT_VAL.sus_fadeIn_time, 2)
			set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
			i := 0
			while(i <= (NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, i + sus_group)
				inc(i)
			end while
			i := 0
			while(i <= NUM_SUSTAIN_FX_GROUPS) 
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, i + sus_fx_group)
				inc(i)
			end while
		end if
	else
		if(num_notes = 1)
			last_note := event_note
			if((1 + sh_right(abs(NUM_ATK_GROUPS) - 1, 31)) = TRUE)
				is_attack := - 1
				wait(90000)
				is_attack := abs(sh_right(abs(NOTE_HELD) - 1, 31))
			else
				is_attack := FALSE
			end if
			set_event_par_arr(ALL_EVENTS, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
			event_id := play_note(note, EVENT_VELOCITY, sus_s_start, - 1)
			set_event_mark(event_id, MARK_1)
			attack_id := play_note(note, CC[103], 0, 0)
			if(btn_sus = TRUE)
				set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
				iii := 0
				while(iii <= (NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
					set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, iii + atk_sus_group)
					inc(iii)
				end while
				iii := 0
				while(iii <= NUM_SUSTAIN_FX_GROUPS) 
					set_event_par_arr(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, iii + sus_fx_group)
					inc(iii)
				end while
				if((1 + sh_right(abs(NUM_ATK_GROUPS) - 1, 31)) = TRUE)
					set_event_par_arr(attack_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, atk_group + rr_count[note])
					rr_count[note] := (rr_count[note] + 1) mod NUM_ATK_GROUPS
				end if
			end if
		else
			note_off(event_id)
		end if
	end if
	last_transition := transition_id
	last_note := event_note
	release_note := - 1
end function

function scan.samples() : Unknown
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_sModInd), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInCurve), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutCurve), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	i := 0
	while(i <= (2000 - 1)) 
		zone_ids_master[i] := - 1
		file_names_master[i] := ""
		inc(i)
	end while
	u := 0
	while(u <= (NUM_TRANS_GROUPS - 1)) 
		ii := range[0]
		while(ii <= range[1]) 
			iii := 1
			while(iii <= 120) 
				wait_longer()
				blip_note := play_note(ii, iii, 0, - 1)
				set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
				change_vol(blip_note, - 2000000, 0)
				set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, trans_group + u)
				wait_longer()
				zone_id := get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
				if((zone_id # - 1) and (zone_id # 0))
					if(search(zone_ids_master, zone_id) = - 1)
						trans_idx := search(zone_ids_master, - 1)
						if(1 = TRUE)
							zone_ids_master[trans_idx] := (sh_left(lsb(abs(trans_group - get_zone_par(get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_GROUP))), 14) .or. sh_left(lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO)), 7)) .or. lsb(get_zone_par(get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY))
						else
							zone_ids_master[trans_idx] := zone_id
						end if
						file_names_master[trans_idx] := get_sample(zone_id, NI_FILE_NAME)
						legatoList.trans_zone_groups[trans_idx] := u
						set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_filename), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, file_names_master[trans_idx])
						set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scanningList), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
						set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_noInput), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
						set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scanningSettings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
					end if
				end if
				fade_out(blip_note, 0, 1)
				iii := iii + 5
			end while
			wait_longer()
			inc(ii)
		end while
		wait_longer()
		inc(u)
	end while
	NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES := search(zone_ids_master, - 1)
	NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED := search(trans_zone_ids, - 1)
	save_array_str(zone_ids_master, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "zone_ids_master.nka")
	save_array_str(file_names_master, legato_path & legato_prefixes[prefix_idx] & "file_names_master.nka")
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scanningList), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_scanningSettings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_noInput), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_sModInd), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseCurve), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInCurve), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutCurve), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_waitTime), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, HIDE_PART_NOTHING)
end function

function update.eqBandwidth() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (search(vibrato_groups, - 1) - 1)) 
		set_engine_par(ENGINE_PAR_BW1, get_ui_id(sli_eqBandwidth), vibrato_groups[i], 5, 1)
		inc(i)
	end while
end function

function legatoSettings.show(Boolean : int) : Unknown
	btn_legatoSettings := Boolean
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_dataSettings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_legatoSettings])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_waveform), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_legatoSettings])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_sustainSettings), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_legatoSettings])
	visibility.resetWindow(FALSE)
	visibility.forallWindow(FALSE)
	reset.label_texts()
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_reset), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_legatoSettings])
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_forall), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_legatoSettings])
end function

function reset.label_texts() : Unknown
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_volume), "Zone Vol.")
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestart), "S. Start")
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_waitSus), "Wait Time")
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_releaseSus), "Release")
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInSus), "Fade In")
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeInTrans), "Fade In")
	set_text(get_ui_id(lbl_fadeOutTrans), "Fade Out")
end function

function update.legatoArrays() : Unknown
	declare z : int
	declare q : int
	z := 0
	while(z <= (2000 - 1)) 
		legatoList.element_numbers[z] := z
		legatoList.trans_file_names[z] := file_names_master[z]
		legatoList.trans_zone_ids[z] := zone_ids_master[z]
		legatoList.marked_elements[z] := 0
		legatoList.intervals[z] := ""
		legatoList.comments[z] := ""
		inc(z)
	end while
	z := 0
	while(z <= (NUM_TRANS_SAMPLES_PLAYED - 1)) 
		q := search(zone_ids_master, trans_zone_ids[z])
		if(q # - 1)
			legatoList.marked_elements[q] := marked_samples[z]
			legatoList.intervals[q] := intervals[z]
			legatoList.comments[q] := sample_comments[z]
		end if
		inc(z)
	end while
end function

function all_windows.show(Boolean : Unknown) : Unknown
	home.show(Boolean)
	settings.show(Boolean)
	legatoSettings.show(Boolean)
	legatoList.show(Boolean)
	vibrato.show(Boolean)
end function

function update.vibIntensity() : Unknown
	sli_vibrato := sli_vibIntensity
	call update.cc_vibrato()
end function

function update.vibrato() : Unknown
	sli_vibIntensity := sli_vibrato
	call update.cc_vibrato()
end function

function release_notes() : Unknown
	if((get_event_mark(release_id, MARK_1) = TRUE) and (event_id = release_id))
		message("release group triggered")
		count := 0
		if(is_attack = FALSE)
			message("no attack")
			release_id := play_note(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE), EVENT_VELOCITY, 0, 0)
			set_event_par_arr(release_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
			i := 0
			while(i <= (NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1)) 
				set_event_par_arr(release_id, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, i + sus_rls_group)
				inc(i)
			end while
		end if
		fade_out(event_id, 200000, 1)
		event_notes[release_note] := - 1
		release_note := event_note
		if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
			call reset.label_texts()
		end if
	end if
end function

function update.gui.legato() : Unknown
	call update.infolabels()
	btn_markSample := marked_samples[trans_idx]
	call update.sampleComment()
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sModRange), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "S. Mod: " & get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_MOD_RANGE))
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_sModInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, (((get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_MOD_RANGE) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_END) - 0)) + 0)
	sli_volume := real_to_int((((int_to_real(trans_event_volume[trans_idx]) - - 10000) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (10000 - - 10000)) + 0)
	sli_samplestart := real_to_int((((((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx]) / 48000) * 1e+06) - 0) * (1e+06 - 0)) / (int_to_real(max_samplestart * 1000) - 0)) + 0)
	call update.zoneVolume()
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestartInd), CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE, real_to_int((((int_to_real(trans_zone_start[trans_idx]) - 0) * (99 - 0)) / (int_to_real(sample_end) - 0)) + 0))
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_samplestart), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, ((((sli_samplestart - 0) * (max_samplestart - 0)) / (1000000 - 0)) + 0) & " ms")
	sli_fadeInTrans := trans_fadeIn_time[trans_idx]
	call update.fadeInTrans()
	sli_fadeOutTrans := trans_fadeOut_time[trans_idx]
	call update.fadeOutTrans()
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_completed), CONTROL_PAR_VALUE, completed_elements[element.idx])
end function

function update.infolabels() : Unknown
	sample_length := get_sample_length(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID))
	sample_end := get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_SAMPLE_END)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(btn_filename), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "File: " & get_sample(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), NI_FILE_NAME))
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_zonevolume), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Vol.: " & get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_VOLUME) & " dB")
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_zonepan), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, "Pan: " & get_zone_par(get_event_par(transition_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_PAN))
	update.played_interval(transition_id)
	playedInterval := midi.note_names[played_interval[0]] & " to " & midi.note_names[played_interval[1]]
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_intervalInfo), CONTROL_PAR_TEXT, playedInterval)
end function

function wait_longer() : Unknown
	wait(900)
end function

function update.cc_dynamics() : Unknown
	set_controller(103, real_to_int((((int_to_real(get_ui_id(sli_dynamics)) - 0) * (127 - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0))
	v := 0
	while(v <= (num_elements(get_ui_id(lbl_sus_filename)) - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_sus_filename[v], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(0 * 2) + 0])
		inc(v)
	end while
	set_control_par(lbl_sus_filename[real_to_int((((int_to_real(sli_dynamics) - 0) * (int_to_real(NUM_DYNAMIC_LAYER - 1) - 0)) / (1e+06 - 0)) + 0)], CONTROL_PAR_FONT_TYPE, _font.2pt7[(1 * 2) + 0])
end function

function update.interval_keycolor(note1 : int, note2 : int) : Unknown
	keys := range[0]
	while(keys <= range[1]) 
		set_key_color(keys, KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
		inc(keys)
	end while
	set_key_color(note1, KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
	set_key_color(note2, KEY_COLOR_BLUE)
end function

function get_keyrange(group_idx : int) : Unknown
	keys := 0
	while(keys <= 127) 
		blip_note := play_note(keys, 1, 0, 1)
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
		change_vol(blip_note, - 2000000, 0)
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, group_idx)
		wait(1)
		zone_id := get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
		if((zone_id # - 1) and (zone_id # 0))
			range[0] := keys
			keys := 127
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note, 0, 1)
		inc(keys)
	end while
	keys := 0
	while(keys <= 127) 
		blip_note := play_note(127 - keys, 1, 0, - 1)
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 0, ALL_GROUPS)
		change_vol(blip_note, - 2000000, 0)
		set_event_par_arr(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ALLOW_GROUP, 1, group_idx)
		wait(1)
		zone_id := get_event_par(blip_note, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID)
		if((zone_id # - 1) and (zone_id # 0))
			range[1] := 127 - keys
			keys := 127
		end if
		fade_out(blip_note, 0, 1)
		inc(keys)
	end while
end function

function update.played_interval(event_id : int) : Unknown
	if((get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO) / 5) <= 12)
		played_interval[0] := get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE) + (get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO) / 5)
		played_interval[1] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY)
	else
		played_interval[0] := get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_NOTE)
		played_interval[1] := get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_ROOT_KEY) + ((get_zone_par(get_event_par(event_id, EVENT_PAR_ZONE_ID), ZONE_PAR_HIGH_VELO) / 5) - 12)
	end if
end function

function get_trans_idx_from_element(result : int, element_idx : Unknown) : int
	if(search(trans_zone_ids, legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element_idx]) = - 1)
		result := search(trans_zone_ids, - 1)
	else
		result := search(trans_zone_ids, legatoList.trans_zone_ids[element_idx])
	end if
end function

function delete.preset() : Unknown
	vibrato_preset[preset_idx.DELETED] := TRUE
	save_array_str(vibrato_preset, base_path & vibPresetNames[mnu_preset] & ".nka")
	ii := 0
	i := 0
	while(i <= (num_elements(vibPresetCount) - 1)) 
		if(i # mnu_preset)
			vibPresetNames[ii] := vibPresetNames[i]
			vibPresetCount[ii] := vibPresetCount[i]
			inc(ii)
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
	save.resource_arrays()
	presetCount := (((presetCount - 1) * (1 + (sh_right(100 - (presetCount - 1), 31) .or. sh_right((presetCount - 1) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((presetCount - 1) - 0, 31))) - (100 * sh_right(100 - (presetCount - 1), 31))
	mnu_preset := (((mnu_preset - 1) * (1 + (sh_right(presetCount - (mnu_preset - 1), 31) .or. sh_right((mnu_preset - 1) - 0, 31)))) - (0 * sh_right((mnu_preset - 1) - 0, 31))) - (presetCount * sh_right(presetCount - (mnu_preset - 1), 31))
	call update.preset.menu()
	if(presetCount # 0)
		load.preset()
	end if
end function

function legatoList.show(Boolean : int) : Unknown
	btn_legatoList := Boolean
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(UI_legatoList), CONTROL_PAR_HIDE, hide_state[btn_legatoList])
	if(- sh_right(abs(development[0] - 22714) - 1, 31) = 1)
		update.legatoArrays()
		update.legatoList()
	end if
end function

function find_key_nka(result : string, array : int[], nka : Unknown, key : int, parent_folder : Unknown, search_depth : int) : string
	declare path : string
	declare it : int
	array[0] := - 1
	it := 0
	path := ""
	_id := load_array_str(array, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR) & path & parent_folder & nka & ".nka")
	while(((_id # - 1) and (it < search_depth)) and (array[0] # key)) 
		array[0] := - 1
		path := path & "../"
		_id := load_array_str(array, get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR) & path & parent_folder & nka & ".nka")
		inc(it)
	end while
	result := get_folder(GET_FOLDER_PATCH_DIR) & path & nka & ".nka"
end function

function update.keycolor() : Unknown
	keys := 0
	while(keys <= 127) 
		set_key_color(keys, KEY_COLOR_INACTIVE)
		if(in_range(keys, range[0], range[1]))
			set_key_color(keys, KEY_COLOR_DEFAULT)
		end if
		inc(keys)
	end while
end function

function init.arrays() : Unknown
	i := 0
	while(i <= (2000 - 1)) 
		if(sus_release_time[i] = 0)
			sus_release_time[i] := DEFAULT_VAL.sus_release_time
		end if
		if(trans_fadeIn_time[i] = 0)
			trans_fadeIn_time[i] := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_fadeIn_time
		end if
		if(trans_fadeOut_time[i] = 0)
			trans_fadeOut_time[i] := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_fadeOut_time
		end if
		if(trans_wait_time[i] = 0)
			trans_wait_time[i] := DEFAULT_VAL.trans_wait_time
		end if
		if(sus_fadeIn_time[i] = 0)
			sus_fadeIn_time[i] := DEFAULT_VAL.sus_fadeIn_time
		end if
		if(trans_zone_ids[i] = 0)
			trans_zone_ids[i] := - 1
		end if
		inc(i)
	end while
end function
